Magic Online Championship Series - 2011 Season 10 QPs Earned
============================================================



 Posted in **Magic Online**
 on April 9, 2009 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











Qualifier Points (QPs) are awarded to Magic Online players based on finishing well in various Magic Online tournaments. For details on how QPs are earned and what you can receive for earning QPs, read the [Magic Online Championship Series Fact Sheet](/en/articles/archive/magic-online-championship-series-2009-05-07).

These are QP points toward Season 10. The Season 10 Championship will be held on September 24 at 11:00 AM PDT, and the promo card is a **full art** version of:

![Dungrove Elder](http://gatherer.wizards.com/Handlers/Image.ashx?size=small&type=card&name=Dungrove%20Elder&options=)This table shows all players who have received 1 or more QPs in Season 10. Points are updated daily at 9:00 PM PDT, with each update adding QPs from events that finished the previous day.
